Fourth Series of Books Continued Reservation

Shanghai Commercial Press published the Fourth Series of Books in the eighth year of the Republic of China. The books collected are all rare and good books that are not seen in the world. Therefore, both editions have sold as many as 5,000 copies. Since its publication, scholars at home and abroad have requested that the sequel be printed for more than ten years. The library has responded to the needs of the times and is preparing to continue the sequel, searching extensively and collecting dozens of hundreds of thousands of volumes of fine manuscripts from the Song, Yuan, Ming, and Qing dynasties. Mr. Zhang Jusheng, a director of the library, also personally went overseas and traveled to the two capitals to seek information. Collectors at home and abroad have produced rare and unusual books for assistance. Before January 28, the library had compiled the complete list of the sequel, which was more beautiful and rich than the first edition. Just as it was about to be sold for reservation, the Japanese army disturbed Shanghai, and the library's general factory and Oriental Library were destroyed. Fortunately, the fine copies included in the sequel were mostly stored in external warehouses and were not completely destroyed. Since the resumption of business, the library has reorganized and started selling reservations for the Fourth Series of Books Sequel on January 15 of this year. It is stipulated that about 10 volumes will be published every week, and 500 volumes will be published every year. It is printed with the beginning of editing and printing, and includes the books planned to be published this year and next year. Those who see this list say that the elites of East Asian collectors are all gathered here. This is not a false reputation. The publication method is also as convenient as the first edition. Those who purchase reservations and those who purchase individual species can view them on schedule first. The books published in January and February, such as the Song Dynasty edition of Mr. Donglai's Poetry Collection, the Song Dynasty edition of the Pingzhai Collection, the Song Dynasty edition of the Kuotanlu, and the Zhuoguge edition of the Huijian Qianlu Houlu Sanlu Yuhua, are all lost books in China, and the only remaining copies in the world. In addition, there are huge productions such as Taiping Yulan and Cefu Yuangui, which were not even prepared by the Ming and Qing dynasties. In addition, the Jiaqing's Revised Unified History, 560 volumes, only has the present copy and has never been printed. Now all of them have been obtained by the library and included in the sequel, which is truly an unprecedented great cause in the East Asian publishing world.

Son Threatens Mother with Gun for Extortion

Purchased a Six-Chambered Old, Rusty Handgun from a Used Goods Stall

Aimed at His Elderly Mother, Who Was Extremely Frightened and Called for Help

He intended to use it to threaten his mother when asking for money. If she refused, he could use the gun to intimidate her, and she would be forced to give him money out of fear. He felt very pleased with himself. One night before, around 9 PM, Afu went home with the gun and demanded money from his mother in a forceful tone. Wang, not understanding his intention, refused. Afu immediately pulled out the handgun from his side, aimed it at his mother, pretending to shoot, in order to threaten and coerce her into giving him several silver dollars. His mother was terrified and screamed for help. Neighbors, hearing the noise, came to inquire. The old woman told them what had happened. Upon learning the truth, the neighbors condemned Afu's actions. Ding Wang had the neighbors help her bind Afu with ropes. She then rushed to the French police station to report that there were robbers in her house committing robbery, requesting them to arrest them immediately. Upon receiving the report, the police chief immediately dispatched a large squad of Chinese and foreign detectives, armed and wearing steel vests, in a police car to rush to the address to surround and capture the suspects. When the detectives arrived at the old woman's house, they saw no trace of robbers, only Afu bound and lying on the ground with the handgun placed on the table. They questioned the old woman and learned the truth: it was her son threatening her with a gun to extort money. They untied Afu and took him and the handgun to the police station for detention. Yesterday, he was escorted to the First Criminal Division of the Special District Court, where Judge Wang Gangxu presided over the hearing. The police lawyer, Yao Zhaodi, presented the case, stating that the police station still needed to conduct a detailed investigation and requested that the defendant be remanded in custody for two weeks for further investigation and interrogation. He also submitted the handgun as evidence. The plaintiff, Ding Wang, then testified about her son's threatening her with a gun and demanding money. Afu's testimony was evasive. The court ordered a further hearing on March 9, and the defendant was remanded in custody.

The Second Collection of Yue Yuan's Secret Manuscript Will Be Published

Widely Collects Lost Sayings of Past Generations

Extensively Gathers Unique Words from Ancient and Modern Times

Compiled into a Rare Secret Manuscript

After the publication of the first collection of Yue Yuan's publications in the Siming Series, scholars across the country regarded it as a model because it extensively collected lost sayings of past generations and gathered unique words from ancient and modern times. Now, Mr. Zhang Yongni has compiled the second collection, extensively gathering rare editions and collecting from classics, culling and adding whatever is sufficient to instruct the world, into 171 volumes, which have already been sent for engraving and are expected to be published next month. The essence of the second collection is even greater than that of the first. Upon investigation, there are countless famous books and records in Siming throughout history, numbering thousands, but more than half have been lost due to the distance of time. Even those that occasionally survive are often unclear due to errors and omissions in the text. For example, Sun Shiyi's "Textual Research on the Extraneous Records," "Collection of Mr. Xuechu," "Record of Hermitage on Bian Mountain," "Remaining Drafts of Qingxi," "Posthumous Collection of Chen Liangmo," "Guo Yiyan," "Complete Collection of Qian Sule," "Special Collection of Xue Weng," "Forbidden Drafts of Yuyi," "Collection of Zhang Huanjing," "Posthumous Writings of Vice Minister Feng," "Posthumous Works of Wang Yi," "Grave Records of the Two Vice Ministers Feng and Wang," "Remaining Affairs of Liujingtang," "Collection of Tunyuezi," "Record of Upright Qi in Xuejiaoting," "Unofficial History of Haidong," "Record of Loyalty and Righteousness in the Song Dynasty," "Ready-Made Words," "Drafts of Supervising Villages," "Chronological Literary Drafts of Qianzhicaotang," "Words of Advice from Cuncaolu," and 22 other kinds, all of which are secretly kept at home. After Mr. Zhang's careful analysis, collection of lost items, and comparison of discrepancies, they have been formed into a unique collection. The set is priced at 50 yuan, and pre-orders are 40 yuan. If both sets are pre-ordered, the price is only 80 yuan. It is sold on behalf of Aiwenyi Road, Jueyuan No. 11.

The Italian Consulate Investigates Two Italians in the Jardine Matheson Fraud Case

Continued Hearing Next Monday

According to the Continental News, Italians Tangbulinis and his son were accused of being involved in the fraud case against Jardine Matheson Bank. Yesterday (February 27), they were interrogated again by the police court of the Italian Consulate. The Russian Aiani and Jiaxing, who have already been convicted in the same case, both testified that Tang had signed checks to withdraw money from the Guohua Bank. The name signed was J. Rice. Tang's son had deposited a fake check for 136,688.25 yuan into the Guohua Bank. Aiani also claimed that Tang's son did not dare to deposit the second fake check for over 188,000 yuan, so Jiaxing took it. Tang received about 5,300 yuan, and his son received 2,800 yuan. Aiani produced a piece of paper with many J. Rice written on it, which Tang had used to practice his signature. Sang Qimu claimed that he went to Puxi Western Firm on January 15 to collect money and personally saw Tang sign a check. The defendants, father and son, denied everything the witnesses said, claiming that they were deliberately framing them. The defendant's lawyer requested permission to hire a calligraphy expert to examine the signature on the check, but the magistrate refused. The hearing was adjourned to next Monday, when the defendant's lawyer will deliver his final arguments, after which the case can be decided. This case involves a total of 12 people: four Russians, three Chinese, one Englishman, one Frenchman, one Portuguese, and two Italians. The Portuguese, Baopuluos Tai, an employee of Jardine Matheson Bank, age 53, will have two witnesses further questioned by the Portuguese Consulate Court today (February 28). After the questioning, the defendant will be sent to the High Court of Macau for trial and punishment.

Crowlae Detained on a Small Boat

Waiting for a Convenient Ship to Send Him Back to the United States

According to the Great American Evening News, Crowlae, who was sentenced two years ago to one year of imprisonment on McLeer Island for smuggling opium from China to various cities on the west coast of the United States, arrived in Shanghai yesterday (February 27) afternoon on the Japanese ship Shanghai Maru. The Passport Management Officer of the Public Security Bureau refused him permission to land because his passport had expired in 1930 and had not been approved by Chinese consular officials in the United States or Japan. The real reason, it is said, is that Crowlae is inherently restless, and it is feared that he will resume opium trafficking in China. The original intention was to send Crowlae back to his point of departure on the same ship, but the crew of the Shanghai Maru refused to take him. Therefore, Crowlae is temporarily detained on a small boat in the Huangpu River, waiting for a convenient ship to send him back to the United States. The reason for detaining him on a small boat is that if he were detained in Nanshi, the Chinese officials would have no right to detain him and would have to hand him over to the US Consulate. It is said that the Public Security Bureau informed the US Consul General in Shanghai in advance. Crowlae was the first person to import ice cream into Shanghai, hence the nickname "Ice Cream Man."

Loss of Property Worth Over a Thousand Yuan

The Robbers Opened Fire, Fortunately No One Was Injured

The other three robbers rushed upstairs to the bedroom of Ling Xiangsheng's mother (Zhang's mother-in-law) in the living room and Zhang's room in the wing. They used kitchen knives to pry open the cabinets and drawers, and robbed more than 300 yuan in cash and a ring, worth more than 500 yuan. They also took a gold ring inlaid with a cat's-eye gemstone, which was deposited by Ms. Xiang Zhilian, who lived in the same lane at No. 2. It was of great value. At that time, the housemaid of the landlord, surnamed Chen, walked back to the drying platform from the grass room upstairs. The robber caught a glimpse of her and grabbed her. The maid screamed for help. The robber was anxious and fired a shot. Fortunately, it did not hit her. The bullet destroyed a hole in the willow Goubi in the east pavilion of the atrium, and the bullet landed in the drainpipe there. The robbers then fled through the main gate. Afterwards, after checking the lost property, the municipal Public Security Bureau, District 1, was notified. At the time, Zhang's wife carried out a pearl necklace that she had borrowed from a relative with the surname of Someone, but it has not been returned, so it was not stolen. Only when Zhang's wife returned home did she find out.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Industry Re-Appeals to the National Government to Establish a Rayon Factory

Requests Reduction of Import Tax Before the Factory Is Established

In order to rescue the critically endangered domestic silk industry, the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Silk Weaving Association submitted a request to the National Government in November of last year to allocate funds to establish a rayon silk factory. However, a long time has passed, and no approval has been received. Therefore, yesterday, they resubmitted it to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the National Economic Commission, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry, requesting that the factory be established quickly. The original text is extracted as follows: "A report is hereby submitted to continue the discussion and sincerely request approval for the rapid establishment of a rayon factory, in order to save the silk industry from the current crisis. The association held a meeting of representatives of the silk industry guilds from the two provinces in January of last year, and resolved to request a loan of 20 million US dollars from the US Cotton Commission to establish a rayon factory to rescue the endangered domestic silk, etc. A special report has been submitted to the case. Now, the silk industry is even more depressed and unsustainable. The number of factories that have closed down is increasing. Even those that survive are in danger of collapsing. Alas, the domestic silk, which is famous for its silk, has such a phenomenon of being on the verge of extinction. What is the reason? The association has investigated the causes and will report them in detail. First, silk merchants adhere to old methods and use all-natural silk for weaving silk, without improving it, resulting in products that are not beautiful in color and are not as pretty as rayon foreign silk, and the price is too high, and sales are not widespread. Because various woven silk fabrics and silk goods made of foreign rayon are sold in abundance, our country's officials and people compete with them because they are pretty and bright in color, and they buy them one after another. As a result, domestic silk has been greatly dwarfed and cannot compete, and it has fallen sharply to the point of being eliminated. Later, enthusiastic people went to foreign countries to investigate and practice silk weaving, and learned all its secrets. After returning to China, they imitated the foreign silk weaving method and also took rayon to interweave into silk. Its beautiful color is indeed similar to that of foreign silk, and the price is low and the quality is good. As a result, the sales gradually expanded, and China's silk industry slightly improved. However, due to natural disasters and man-made disasters, foreign aggression and internal strife, traffic congestion has come one after another, and rayon imports have been repeatedly taxed, resulting in high costs of domestic silk, which is not as good as foreign silk, resulting in a slump in business. Moreover, the Eastern neighbors do not tax the import of foreign rayon, which is higher than the tax in our country, so the cost of Eastern silk is light, and our silk merchants have to buy heavily taxed rayon raw materials to make silk, and the price of silk is naturally expensive. Comparing the two, the difficulty of selling is self-evident. No wonder China's silk industry is on the verge of failure. However, if we want to protect the survival and revival of domestic silk, it is important to establish our own rayon factory, study the products carefully, and produce a large amount for national needs. Otherwise, the silk will be even more chaotic, and domestic silk will not be able to survive. The association held a meeting of representatives of silk industry guilds from the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang this month to discuss the relief of the silk industry and jointly studied the matter. It was resolved that: (1) We will continue to submit a request to the government to establish a rayon factory as soon as possible, in order to provide fundamental relief. (2) Before a rayon factory is established, we should increase the import tax on rayon in order to reduce the cost of domestic silk, so that it will not be sold by foreign silk, and we should increase the import tax on foreign rayon woven products in order to mix with domestic silk. The association investigated that rayon silk has almost become a necessary raw material for weaving silk, and there is no possibility of eliminating it. It is necessary to find a way to make it ourselves and use it as much as possible, in order to save the silk from danger, and both the national economy and people's livelihood will benefit. It is not something that can be resisted by taxation. The higher the rayon tax rate, the heavier the cost of domestic silk and the slower the sales, the easier it is for foreign silk to be sold, and the more foreign silk is sold, the more domestic silk is defeated. The association, in order to maintain the livelihood of workers in silk weaving factories in the two provinces, hereby follows the weaving and submits a report to respectfully request the National Government (Yuan, Council, Ministry) to approve and implement it, and we are eagerly awaiting orders.

Loss Less Than Ten Yuan

No Negotiation with Sanbei

Dr. Zhang Sumin's Talk on the Silver Price Issue

Dr. Zhang Sumin, Director of the Banking Department of National Jinan University, gave a speech yesterday on the silver price issue, saying that there is a strong voice in the US Congress to raise the price of silver. Some advocate setting the gold-silver ratio at 1:20, and some even advocate setting the ratio at 1:12. Today's market price is 1:70. If the silver price is artificially raised several times, it will undoubtedly disrupt China's exchange rate and commodity prices. There are two ways for our country to defend itself: First, implement an export tax on silver, with the tax rate depending on the extent to which the US government raises the price of silver. The effect of this method is equivalent to prohibiting the export of silver, but not as drastic. However, it is necessary to prevent the smuggling of silver and Chinese banks' depositors from withdrawing cash and depositing it in foreign banks at the same time. Second, the Chinese government should not only allow people to transport silver out, but also transport it out in large quantities to buy US dollars or gold bars as a basis for changing the monetary standard. At the same time, it must decouple domestic currency from the silver standard. I think these methods are all worthy of research, but their relationship is complex and cannot be easily explained.

Seventy-First Time

The seventy-first inspection report of the Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee of the Shanghai Bank of China stated that the committee members and the entrusted accountants, based on the rules of the committee, inspected the issuance of Shanghai Bank of China's head office and the exchange voucher reserve vault used by the branch banks. The seventy-second inspection was held at the bank on February 25, 1934, and the director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance joined the inspection. The inspection results are listed on the left: The total amount of exchange vouchers issued was 11,951,719,931 yuan, including 76,353,053 yuan issued by the head office, 21,088,054 yuan used by the branch banks, and 22,070,684 yuan used by the various banks. Except for the portion used by the various banks, which is inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection of the portion used by the branch banks is as follows: The amount issued by the head office and used by the branch banks is 97,441,107 yuan. The amount of exchange voucher reserves for the head office and branch banks is 97,441,107 yuan, including 60,200,634.43 yuan in cash reserves and 37,234,757.57 yuan in security reserves. The above two items, the cash reserves account for 60% and the security reserves account for 40%, are all checked and found to be correct. According to Article 5 of the rules, this is a formal report. February 25, 1934, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, Da Kan, representatives of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Wang Yansong and Pei Yun, representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association Tang Shoumin and Hu Yang'an, representatives of the Shanghai Currency Association Wang Huai Kang and Qian Zusheng, representatives of the voucher-receiving banks Zhang Wu and Lin Rongsheng, directors and supervisors of the Bank of China Chen Guangfu, Xu Jiqing, and Li Zhilian, accountant Wang Zikang.

Reading Q&A

Where Should One Start When Studying International Issues? (3)

When studying international issues, first, we should stand from the perspective of historical materialism and pay special attention to the economic background. All international phenomena are reflections of global economic changes. Studying today's international issues without considering the capitalist economic system and its dynamics is just wishful thinking. To understand recent international events, we must understand the characteristics of the economic panic in the third period of capitalism. Capitalism's attempt to ease economic panic and political crises through mutual compromise had suffered a final defeat in 1933. Consequently, 1934 naturally entered a stage of more blatant preparation for war. On this basis, there will inevitably be the Paris massacre, the street fighting in Austria, the US buying up silver, the arms race, secret treaties, and the conclusion of alliances. At the same time, they will jointly launch an offensive against China and jointly deploy an anti-Soviet war. All of this constitutes the current international situation, and its foundation lies in the collapse of the capitalist economy. The direction of the world economy has turned to a new direction. This is the root of all international disputes and the clue to analyzing international issues.

First, we should study from the fluidity of the past, the unity of contradictions. The occurrence of each international event is a product of a certain stage in the process and is also contradictory, mutually opposed, and unified within a certain category. All international phenomena have certain cause-and-effect relationships, which are continuous movements. We can only obtain the truth about international issues in a dynamic state. For example, let's talk about the League of Nations. The League of Nations was originally an organization for Anglo-French-Italian-Japanese power chauvinists to carve up small nations, colonies, and suppress world revolutions. It has been developing until now, and although its essence has not changed, this organization currently has the role of preventing Germany's fascist challenge. In a certain sense, it temporarily has the value of existence. If you don't see this point and shout to overthrow the League of Nations at this time, it is tantamount to helping the German National Socialist Party and accelerating the outbreak of imperialist war. For example, now that the Austrian Socialist Party has failed, it is completely wrong to see it as the political stability of the Austrian bourgeoisie. The failure of the Socialist Party naturally has its objective reasons. The main reason is that its political program cannot win the support of the masses. Although a large number of people participated in this bloodshed, the leadership could not be unified, which dispersed the power of the mass camp and did not match the government's restraining force. But has the revolution been suppressed? Not necessarily. The failure of the Socialist Party this time may have gathered the masses to unify under stronger and more correct leadership, and from then on embarked on the possibility of more tenacious hand-to-hand combat. Moreover, the occurrence of the Austrian incident is precisely due to the sharpening of the opposition between the rich and poor groups, which is a necessary phenomenon in the process of capitalist decline and cannot be said to be a victory for the dictatorship of a minority. Therefore, we can only explore its development process to understand the truth of the Austrian incident.

Third, we should pay attention to studying from the perspective of connections. That is to say, there is no international event in the world now that is completely unrelated to others. China's "bandit" suppression seems to be a Chinese problem that has nothing to do with others, but in fact, the British Parliament is very concerned, and countries such as the United States, France, and Japan dare not take it lightly. This is because China is everyone's market. If the market is not stable, it will affect their trade, production, labor-capital struggles, unemployment, social disorder, and even the collapse of capitalism.

The above are just a few principles. To correctly study international issues, you must naturally have a considerable understanding of social sciences. In particular, you should have a correct understanding of economics and historical materialism. In addition, you must be able to apply these principles to practice. This is a more difficult problem. If you don't use the methods well, you naturally can't have a correct estimate. If there are problems with the methods, it will be even more irrelevant. (Regarding this issue, there is a book in the Self-Study Series on how to self-study international issues, which will be published next month and can be used for reference. I won't go into detail here).

(3) A person who does not understand foreign languages can also study international issues, but the scope of research materials will be narrower. However, it is more difficult if you don't understand economics, because a researcher should at least understand the structure and dynamics of the capitalist economy, otherwise it is difficult to get started. As for how to satisfy your desires, you can only spend some time reading a few of the most basic and reliable books on economic theory, or discuss preliminary knowledge of economics with friends who understand economics!

4. It would take a long time to say where to start studying economics, so I'll have to talk about it when there is an opportunity. Fortunately, this department will soon publish a book on research methods for this type of book, which can be distributed. Before publication, I think you can also refer to the article "Preliminary Reading Methods of Social Sciences" published in the Reading Q&A column of this newspaper on February 21, 22, and 23.

In addition, pay special attention to collecting research materials. The sources of information naturally come from "reading newspapers" and "reading magazines," but most newspapers and magazines have a background. You must be able to distinguish which imperialist organization a news agency is the mouthpiece of and which political position a magazine takes as its background. If you don't know the source of the material and the role of the propaganda machine, even if you have the correct research methods, it will still be useless.

We are very happy that you are not ashamed to ask questions, and we welcome you to write to us again to discuss any points that are unclear or unsatisfactory after reading this article. We also ask you and all readers to criticize our opinions frankly.

Ministry of Education Dispatches Personnel to Inspect Specialized Schools Above the College Level in Jinan and Tianjin

(Nanjing, 28th) The Ministry of Education dispatched Chen Yazhong, Sun Guofeng, Guo Youshou, Liu Yingshi, Hao Gengsheng, and others on the 28th to inspect specialized schools above the college level in Jinan, Tianjin, Beiping, Baoding, Kaifeng, Wuhan, Changsha, and Anqing. Hunan Education Director Zhu Jingnong Talks About Hunan Education

Hunan Education Director Zhu Jingnong came to Beijing a few days ago to discuss middle and primary school regulations and entrance examination regulations with the Ministry of Education and report on education matters in the province. He went to the Ministry of Education on the afternoon of the 27th and met with various officials of the Ministry to discuss matters. Because of our friendship, the reporter casually talked about education in Hunan. A brief summary is as follows: (1) There are many schools in Hunan Province. There are more than 23,000 primary schools with more than 840,000 students. There are 170 middle schools (including all levels of vocational schools) with more than 30,000 students. There is one university in Hunan for higher education with more than 500 students. The number of students in private Xiangya Medical College and Qunzhi College of Law and Politics varies from one to two hundred. (2) Education funding: universities receive more than 300,000 yuan, and the actual expenditure on education in the province is 1.8 million yuan. However, there is a lot of local education funding, which amounts to more than 9 million yuan when calculated together. (3) Vocational education: there are nine provincial vocational schools, including two senior schools (one agriculture and one industry) and seven junior schools (six male schools and one female school). There are many vocational schools run by local and private individuals, with more than 100 schools. (4) Normal education: there is one independent normal school, and six schools (three male and three female) have normal departments in middle schools. There are many rural normal schools. There are currently sixty rural normal schools in 75 counties in the province. The trend in the province is to develop joint rural normal schools as much as possible, because joint schools in several counties can concentrate talent and economy better than individual schools in each county. The three counties formerly under Yuanzhou have now been united to establish a joint rural normal school. The five counties formerly under Yuezhou are also jointly establishing a joint rural normal school, which is currently being piloted. (5) Social education: The provincial popular education center runs a popular newspaper with wide sales of tens of thousands of copies. The farmer education center runs three experimental zones: the western zone is centered on Hunan University, the southern zone is centered on Xiuye Agricultural School, and the northern zone is centered on the people's education center itself. It experiments with culture (short-term free education for adults and remedial education), agriculture (improving agriculture and introducing farmers), autonomy, sanitation, and other work. Each county has a district library, all of which have Wan You Wen Ku.

Ministry of Education Pays Attention to Physical Examinations for Government-Funded Students Studying Abroad Due to American Notification that Many Chinese Students Studying in the US Have Tuberculosis

Yesterday's Announcement of Measures for Physical Examinations of Government-Funded Students Studying Abroad

The Ministry of Education approved a consultation from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating that it had received a note from the US Embassy Office in Beijing, stating, "Recently, there have been many cases of students from various countries developing tuberculosis while studying in the United States. This disease was latent when these students applied for visas, and once it develops after entering school in the US, it often causes many difficulties and requires a lot of money. This is because those suffering from this disease do not seek immediate treatment before departing for the US. According to US law, students sent to the US by foreign governments do not need to present a physical examination certificate to obtain a government-funded student visa. However, government-funded students should undergo the same examinations as other students, with special attention paid to whether there is latent tuberculosis. The US Embassy hereby requests the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to instruct its subordinate agencies to inform government-funded students applying for passports to the US about this matter. The relevant authorities of the US government plan to implement this measure, that all government-funded students, regardless of nationality, must undergo examinations. Students applying for visas are generally examined by doctors designated by the relevant US consular officials. For government-funded students from your country, only a written statement from a US consular official or a doctor designated by your Ministry of Education is required for recognition." In addition to notifying the various passport issuing agencies, it is appropriate to consult for reference. After approving the consultation, the Ministry of Education specially formulated five articles of measures for the physical examination of government-funded students selected by provinces and cities yesterday, and instructed all colleges and universities above junior college level, as well as the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, to comply. The order stated, "It is hereby ordered that all provinces and cities must conduct physical examinations for students selected for government-funded study abroad, as stipulated in the Ministry's regulations for studying abroad. In order to effectively implement this, five items of physical examination measures for government-funded students selected by provinces and cities have been specially formulated. When selecting government-funded students for study abroad in various countries in the future, these must be followed. In addition to distributing copies, a copy of the measures is attached for the information of the 'Departments,' 'Bureaus,' and 'Schools,' and to inform the students accordingly."

Attached: Measures for Physical Examination of Government-Funded Students Selected by Provinces and Cities (1) When provinces and cities hold selections for government-funded students studying abroad, they should conduct physical examinations for all candidates in accordance with the provisions of Article 11 of the Regulations for Studying Abroad. (2) The physical examination in the preceding paragraph shall be conducted by qualified hospitals or doctors designated by the education departments and bureaus of the respective provinces and cities. The physical examination form must be signed by the hospital or doctor to be valid. (3) The education departments and bureaus of the respective provinces and cities shall submit two copies of the physical examination forms of the candidates who passed the preliminary examination, along with the documents stipulated in Article 13 of the Regulations for Studying Abroad, to the Ministry for review. (4) If the Ministry deems it necessary to re-examine the physical examination forms of the candidates who passed the preliminary examination, it may order the candidate to undergo a re-examination at a designated hospital or doctor. (5) After the Ministry has reviewed and approved the physical examination forms of all candidates, one copy will be kept by the Ministry for future reference, and the other copy will be stamped with the word "Examined" by the Ministry and issued to the candidates along with the certificate of passing the re-examination for their receipt.

Ministry of Education Orders Submission of Film Scripts to the Central Propaganda Committee for Review

(Nanjing, 28th) The Ministry of Education has received an order that the Central Propaganda Committee, in order to guide the film industry and encourage talented individuals to write film scripts, has specially formulated measures for the review and registration of film scripts. Overview of Study Abroad Education in Jiangxi Province

(Nanchang Correspondence) In Jiangxi Province, in the 20th year of the Republic [1931], there were 107 students studying in Japan, 7 in Germany, 8 in France, 4 in England, 10 in the US, 0 in Belgium, 0 in Switzerland, for a total of 136. In the 21st year of the Republic [1932], there were 80 in Japan, 13 in Germany, 13 in France, 2 in England, 5 in the US, 1 in Belgium, 1 in Switzerland, for a total of 116. In the 20th year of the Republic, there were 90 government-funded students, 1 semi-government-funded student, 9 with subsidies, 36 with grants, and 0 self-funded, for a total of 136. In the 21st year of the Republic, there were 71 government-funded students, 4 semi-government-funded students, 2 with subsidies, 23 with grants, and 16 self-funded, for a total of 116. Regarding subjects of study, in the 20th year of the Republic, there were 32 in Arts, 22 in Engineering, 22 in Law, 18 in Science, 10 in Education, 10 in Medicine, 6 in Commerce, 2 in Agriculture, and 7 in other fields, for a total of 136. In the 21st year of the Republic, there were 26 in Arts, 24 in Engineering, 9 in Law, 23 in Science, 8 in Education, 6 in Medicine, 10 in Commerce, 2 in Agriculture, 3 in Art, and 5 in other fields, for a total of 116. According to the above: (1) Due to the influence of Japanese oppression, the number of students studying in Japan has decreased, while the number of students studying in Germany and France has increased. (2) The number of government-funded students has decreased due to the difficulty of selection, while the number of self-funded students has increased sharply. (3) The number of students studying Arts and Law has decreased, while the number studying Science and Commerce has slightly increased.

He Siyuan, Director of the Shandong Education Department (He has other matters to discuss with the Ministry of Education), along with the members of this year's Shandong inspection group to Europe and Chen Jianheng (Education Commissioner dispatched by the Shandong Provincial Government to inspect education in Europe and America), Dong Huai (Director of the Shandong Provincial People's Education Museum) and his wife Ms. Kong Fanduo, Xu Yiqian (Principal of the Shandong Provincial Fourth Normal School), Sun Weiyue (Principal of the Shandong Provincial First Middle School), and five others, arrived in Beijing on the 26th and stayed at the Central Hotel. The Sixth Standing Committee Meeting of the Children's Welfare Association Plans to Build Nurseries in Nanshi and Zhabei

Relief for Poor and Homeless Children

Construction Costs Tentatively Set at Sixty Thousand Yuan

Children's Day to be Prepared by the Education Bureau and Others

The Mayor Will Also Host All Children in the City

The Shanghai Children's Welfare Association held its sixth standing committee meeting at the Municipal Government Reception Office on Xiafei Road the night before last. The attendees included Wu Tiecheng, President of the Association, standing committee members Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Chen Heqin, Hu Shuli, Wang Guanyi, Zhao Zengqi, and Wen Hongen (representing Yin Guanzhi), Yang Maorong, and Zhou Wanghe. Wu Tiecheng chaired the meeting, and Hu Shuyi recorded the minutes. The details are as follows:

Matters Reported

The heads of the Association's four departments, the Children's Protection Department, the Research Department, the Health Department, and the Business Department, reported on the progress of their respective departments as follows: A. Children's Protection Department: (1) The department's address is temporarily located in the First Nursery. (2) During the opening and trial operation period, Wang Yiting and Wen Hongen, the directors, will be responsible for fundraising. (3) The scope of work is temporarily set at five items: (1) Investigating the treatment of child laborers. (2) Assisting local governments in prohibiting the enslavement of children, investigating abused children. (3) Rescuing abducted children. (4) Providing shelter for abandoned children and rescuing homeless children. (4) Ensuring the safety of children outdoors. (4) The business undertaking will be trialed for three months first, with funding provided by the Municipal Public Security Bureau and Mr. Wang Yiting. Whether or not to expand will be determined based on the results. (5) Passing the rules of procedure. B. Children's Research Department: (1) Formulating the department's research plan. (2) Devising a normal child health scale. C. Children's Health Department: (1) Planning to establish infant health guidance centers in Nanshi and Zhabei, one in each location. (2) Planning to organize a summer camp this summer. D. Children's Business Department: (1) Deciding to first establish a nursery. The municipal government has allocated a public property near Panfang as the public address of the Association's First Nursery. (2) Passing the rules of procedure for the nursery business group committee. (3) Passing the regulations for the operation of type A nurseries.

Important Cases Resolved

(1) The Association will build one large-scale labor nursery each in Nanshi and Zhabei in the near future. In the future, the labor nurseries will serve as the center for rescuing poor and homeless children in the northern and southern cities, with the aim of gradually extending this to the entire city. (2) Please ask Pan Gongzhan and Chang Maolao to contact the Municipal Land Bureau and the Municipal Public Works Bureau to find suitable public properties and land for the construction of the labor nurseries. (3) Please ask Li Ting'an, Chen Heqin, and Hu Shuyi to design the construction plan for the labor nurseries and submit it to the Standing Committee for discussion. (4) The construction cost for the labor nurseries is tentatively set at sixty thousand yuan. (6) Fundraising methods for the construction of labor nurseries. (Omitted) (7) On March 15, President Wu will host the members of the city's Children's Day at the Municipal Government Reception Office on Xiafei Road. The Second Issue of Volume VII of the Law Journal is Published

The Law Journal, published by the Dongwu Law School, has rich content and is highly praised by scholars at home and abroad. It also publishes special issues from time to time, focusing on a specific legal issue. Last year, it published a special issue on labor law, which was especially appreciated by the general public. In view of the importance of legal education, it has published the first part of a special issue on legal education in the second issue of Volume VII, which has now been published. The content is even more exciting, including Qiu Hanping's "Legal Education and Modernity," Yan Shutang's "The Purpose of Legal Education," Sun Xiaolou's "Several Important Issues in Legal Education in China," Yang Zhaolong's "The Weaknesses of Legal Education in China and Their Remedies," Zhao Chen's "The Task of Criminal Law and the Education of Its Auxiliary Sciences," Liang Jingzhao's translation of "The New Plan for Legal Education," Yang Peng's "Legal Education in Germany," Ling Qihan's "Legal Education in Belgium," Zhao Yingnian's translation of "Legal Education in Japan," Ji Fusheng's "The Judiciary and Legal Education of Siam," Yao Fuguo's translation of "An Overview of Legal Education in South and Central America," Wang Wenmo's "Legal Education in Rome," and Sheng Zhenwei's "Dongwu Legal Education in the Past Nineteen Years." Finally, it also includes several tables, such as the Regulations on the Establishment of Private Law and Political Schools Chartered by the Judicial Yuan, the Contribution of Graduates of Dongwu Law School to Legal Education, and a List of All Universities and Colleges that have Established Law Departments in the Country. This special issue is sold separately for five dimes per copy, and the annual subscription for six issues, including postage, is two yuan. Stamps are accepted. Those who wish to purchase it can contact the Dongwu Law Journal at No. 146 Kunshan Road in this city. Furthermore, the third issue of Volume VII of the journal will be the second part of the special issue on legal education. Domestic jurists such as Dong Kang, Liu Shifang, Qiu Fenling, Yao Qizhou, Lu Jun, Xu Xiangshu, and Ai Guofan have all written treatises on legal education in China and around the world. It is reported that it is currently in print and is expected to be published in mid-March.

Letter from the General Assembly of Provincial Primary and Secondary Schools and Social Education Institutions in Fujian Province

A letter from the General Assembly of Provincial Primary and Secondary Schools and Social Education Institutions in Fujian Province states: Dear Editor, I have read the education news in your newspaper on February 20, with the headline "Fujian Education Sector Demands Repayment of Old Debts from the Puppet Government, Chen Yi Believes It is an Outrageous Action" and the sub-headline "Out of Consideration, Abolish Past Years' Debts and Advance the February Expenses by Half a Month." After investigation, this does not match the facts. The situation is briefly clarified and corrected as follows:

When Zheng Zhenwen took over as Director of the Education Department in November of the 21st year of the Republic [1932], during Director Cheng Shimei's tenure, the education expenses were only short by half a month. Director Cheng served as the Director of Education in Fujian for four years, and the expenses owed for half a month were very limited. Director Zheng, in terms of law and reason, could not ignore the debt simply because it was owed during Cheng's tenure. As for Zheng's tenure from November of the 21st year of the Republic to November of the 22nd year of the Republic [1933], he accumulated more than two months of debt. After the establishment of the puppet government, the schools maintained themselves by borrowing money, and the teachers and staff worked with empty stomachs for another two months. Therefore, including the previous debt, there were more than four months of debt in total. Even if Director Zheng ignored the efforts of the education sector and the fact that the schools borrowed money to maintain themselves during the puppet government period, what reasons would he base his decision to cancel the debts prior to November of the 22nd year of the Republic on? This is the first point. When the principals and staff representatives of the provincial schools negotiated the debts before February 8, they only asked the education authorities to be responsible for economizing expenses or to wait until the government's finances were slightly better before gradually repaying them. There was absolutely no outrageous action. This is what all social figures in Fujian saw and heard. However, Director Zheng neglected his duties. After the departmental meeting on the afternoon of the 8th, he used dangerous words to confuse the situation. Chairman Chen detained the representatives Huang Xianming and Rao Shibin at the Provincial Public Security Bureau at midnight on the 8th. Afterwards, he pushed all the responsibility onto Chairman Chen. His illegal and unreasonable, insidious and despicable actions, trampling on human rights and insulting personal dignity, are now being reported to the Ministry of Education of the National Government by all provincial schools and staff in Fujian Province, hoping to obtain the final judgment of justice and fairness. This is the second point. After Zheng Zhenwen took office as Director of the Education Department of Fujian, he often sent news reports on educational facilities to the Shanghai newspapers for publication. However, in reality, they are far from the propaganda materials.

Regarding the above points, please still publish them in your newspaper's education news column. Sincerely, the Editorial Department of Shen Bao, the General Assembly of Provincial Primary and Secondary Schools and Social Education Institutions in Fujian Province, February 25.

Liu Fuzong Must Work Hard in the Third Sino-British Cue Sports Match

Against Englishman Ge Ling at 5:30 pm

Yesterday Shen Lince Lost Eighteen Points

China Still Leads by Four Hundred and Six Points

In the second Sino-British International Cue Sports Competition, Shen Lince competed against Nie Keer yesterday. Shen won first but lost later. In the competition of seven hundred and fifty points, he lost eighteen points. After the two matches, China still leads by four hundred and six points. Today, in the third match, China's Liu Fuzong will compete against England's Ge Ling. The competition will begin at 5:30 pm. Both players have good skills, and the final outcome will depend on each individual's efforts.

Shen Lince Leads with Excellent Skills

Shen started off well, with thirty-one points on the third shot and thirty-seven points on the seventh shot. After two fluent and refreshing high scores were revealed, Shen had surpassed fifty points. By the tenth shot, Nie Keer suddenly scored fifty-one points with one hand, and the situation of both sides was balanced, fluctuating by about ten points. Based on the prediction of various shooting methods in the future, Shen, with his versatility, was more confident. Sure enough, every shot he made was successful. When it came to the fortieth shot, Shen led by a score of 457 to 353, a difference of two hundred and four points, with high scores of 21, 39, 68, 21, 21, 25, and 22. This was Shen's golden age.

Nie Keer Reverses with Full Endurance

The goal is seven hundred and fifty points, a huge number that cannot be reached in a short time. In addition to skills and experience, it also requires endurance as a backing. At this time, Shen gradually showed signs of fatigue and felt increasingly unsustainable. Nie Keer, however, was not like that. With full endurance, he continued to generate scores of 47, 20, 65, 50, 23, 38, and 30, reaching the goal first. Shen also scored 38, 25, 26, 24, and 24, but his energy was exhausted and he failed. In the end, he lost by a score of 732 to 750.

The Municipal No. 1 Stadium Revises the Regulations for the Amateur Basketball Association

The fourth amateur basketball competition organized by the Municipal No. 1 Stadium will begin registration on March 3rd. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. The newly drafted regulations of the association are listed below:

1. The purpose of this association is to promote amateur sports among industrial and commercial circles, strengthen physical fitness, and improve skills.

2. This association will hire three committee members to manage the association's affairs.

3. All amateur basketball teams from industrial and commercial circles can join this association, but the teams must not include students or physical education teachers (the qualification restrictions are detailed in the amateur qualification regulations for various competitions at this stadium). If this is violated, once discovered, the team's competition qualification will be immediately revoked, and they will never be allowed to participate in any competitions at this stadium.

4. Each team is limited to twelve players, and each person is only allowed to join one team. The joining procedures are detailed in the registration form.

5. Once a team is registered, they cannot change players or increase or decrease the number of people. When registering, a six-inch photo of all team members must be submitted. Those without photos or with photos without names will not be allowed to participate in the competition.

6. Registration will be from March 3rd to March 25th.

7. The competition rules will be implemented according to the latest rules of the Chinese National Sports Association.

8. The competition location will be the outdoor basketball court at this stadium. The balls used for the competition will be provided by the association. The referees for the competition will be hired by the association. The competition dates and times will be scheduled by the association.

9. Teams that are more than ten minutes late for the scheduled competition time will be considered to have forfeited. If both teams are not present, both will be considered to have forfeited. A team that forfeits twice will have its competition qualification revoked. Once the competition qualification is revoked, all previous competitions will also be considered invalid.

10. The competition dates are set for Saturday afternoons and all day Sunday. Each team must arrive at the stadium on time according to the schedule arranged by this association and must not be late. Whether or not there will be a postponement due to rain can be inquired by calling Zhang Longhai at 21089 in Nanshi. If a team has a special reason and wants to reschedule the competition, they must first obtain the consent of the opposing team and jointly submit a letter to the association two days in advance. It will only be effective after being approved by the association.

11. The competition method will be a single round-robin system (if there are many teams, they will be divided into groups according to their skill level, and each group will hold a single round-robin competition). The winner gets one point, and the loser gets zero points. After the round-robin is over, if two teams have the same score, a tie-breaker will be held. If three or more teams have the same score, the knockout competition method will be used to determine the championship.

12. If a team or player is reported or discovered by an association staff member to have violated the competition rules, and after investigation it is confirmed, the result of that competition will be considered a failure, regardless of the outcome. In severe cases, the entire team's competition qualification will be revoked. The same penalties apply to those who exhibit barbaric behavior during the competition and refuse to obey the referee's decisions.

13. Players without numbers on their jerseys will not be allowed to play.

14. Teams must not protest on the spot during the competition or suspend the competition for any reason. The protest letter should be submitted to the committee of this association within two days after the fact. Whether the reasons for the protest are sufficient will be notified by this association in writing, but the decision of the committee is the final judgment, and the protesting team may not object again.

15. These regulations are valid from the start of registration to the end date. If there are any unaddressed matters, they may be proposed for amendment by the committee.

Page 16

Spring and Autumn

Spring Snow

— Yin Qiu

I remember the old saying: "It's hard to be the sky in April, needing both warmth and cold." Because the weather in April is when the wheat ears are growing, requiring coldness, while it's also the silkworm raising season, and silkworms need warmth. If it's suitable for the wheat, it harms the silkworms; if you protect the silkworms, you sacrifice the wheat. You can't have both, so it's really not easy being the sky god in April!

It's still early spring now, not yet April, so it seems being the sky wouldn't be difficult, but in fact, it's not easy either. Because in this February weather, a great spring chill suddenly brews, and in some places, it even snows heavily. Spring chill is a common thing, as the saying goes, "Spring chill freezes old yellow cows to death." The old saying "On the eighth day of the second month, the birthday of Emperor Zhang, eat frozen dog meat" doesn't it all show the harm of spring chill? But it's okay if it doesn't snow, once it snows, trouble comes.

The thing about snow is that it has to fall at the right time, appropriately. Snow falling in the twelfth month is called "winter snow," and it's beneficial without harm, the heavier the better. Pests in the fields all freeze to death, and next year's farming will be smooth, a sign of a bountiful year. That's "auspicious snow." Once spring arrives, if it snows, it's called "spring snow." Spring snow harms spring crops, and is detrimental to farmland. So this time, the sky, by snowing in the spring, has earned many complaints from farmers.

It's said that last year the weather was favorable, the harvests were abundant, yet the rural villages went bankrupt, and the farmers cried in bitterness. The sky god didn't offer relief, but instead sent snow that harmed the crops. If this year is struck with disaster, and the fields are desolate, that would be unthinkable. So the spring snow shows the sky's lack of consideration, the sky's lack of sensitivity. Anything that lacks consideration and sensitivity, whether it's people or the sky, deserves to be scolded. It's only right.

Don't just talk about snow, it needs to fall appropriately; the same goes for rain. If it falls at the right time, it's "timely rain." Rain after a long drought is even called "sweet dew." Conversely, if it doesn't fall at the right time, it's either "torrential rain" or "downpour." I hope the sky god will realize its mistake, atone for its crimes, and send down "sweet rain" to make up for the transgression of the "spring snow." May torrential rain not come, may downpours not be seen, benefiting farming and bestowing kindness on the common people. I know those who blamed the sky will surely praise it, those who hated the sky will surely be grateful to it.

Being the sky is hard, but being human is even harder. Everything you do must be without resentment from others; every word and action must be praised by others. Where virtue reaches, where does hate come from? It also lies in seeking what is suitable for the time, and bestowing kindness on the masses.

The Old Professor

— Shou Cheng

The old professor pushed up the thick glasses that were about to fall off his nose, and shouted in a hoarse voice. The veins on his neck were bulging tightly, and the sparse, gray-yellow beard around his lips twitched as his mouth opened and closed.

The tense emotions of the entire classroom of young people were focused on his waving, shaking fingers｜｜This place was filled with his lifelong dedication, passion, and high hopes. He explained painstakingly, once, twice, repeating tirelessly. Ignoring his own hoarseness, regardless of his own exhaustion, his only wish was that no student would be willing to be vague about understanding anything.

Occasionally, he caught sight of students whispering or gazing idly out the window. Then he would be furious, calling them good-for-nothings and blockheads, stamping his feet and scolding loudly. But not long after, he would approach the classmates he had just reprimanded, stroking their soft hair with his thin, withered hand, warning them with kindness and sincerity: Child, don't hate me. It's for your future that I scold you!

Each time, when he finished teaching a section, he would always lean close to the students, asking with sincere hope: Do you understand? Do you understand? Only when everyone nodded, indicating a clear understanding of everything he had taught, would he smile with satisfaction. But in the end, he would still declare: Don't deceive me! This is easy to understand, as long as you are willing to put your heart into it.

Sometimes, he would happily boast about his knowledge and experience, but after a while, he would change his tone and say: I'm old, useless now! You are young, work hard! I hope that each of you will be stronger than this old man in the future!

Whether in bitter cold or sweltering heat, even when afflicted with illness, he always brought his briefcase to school to teach. Once, a classmate said to him: Sir, you are not in good health, you should rest for a while! But he replied: I have the great responsibility of shaping young people, how dare I be absent arbitrarily! If I neglect your studies, how can I face the expectations of your parents!

His sleeves were always covered with white chalk dust, and the cover of the obscure and worn book he carried under his arm had long lost its vibrant colors; but the spirit of our old professor is forever as strong as the sun!

Random Notes

— Zhao Tingfang

Mr. S. lectured on Chinese language and literature, lecturing on Guo Moruo's new poem ｜｜｜"The universe after the rain, like a conscience washed by tears." He suddenly raged: "What kind of talk is this? Utterly ridiculous! Tears are in the eyes, the heart is in the belly, separated by a layer of skin, how can they be connected together? Truly absurd! Ha! Tears can even wash the heart!"

○ ○ ○

When I was a child, the teacher in the private school taught couplets. I was naturally mischievous, so he often gave me difficult problems to solve. If I didn't do well, he would surely beat me. One day, he gave me a five-character couplet: "People love fat hen." I thought for a long time. Although I could barely come up with an answer, I didn't dare to say it. I couldn't help but laugh and cry. When it was time to dismiss in the evening, he called me over and scolded: "Mischievous thing!" Is this little thing so hard to answer? You can answer with "I follow the fat woman"!" I couldn't help but burst out laughing, spraying snot on the teacher's desk. The teacher also smiled slightly and said, "Go!"

○ ○ ○

Many new novelists flaunt themselves as symbolic, romantic, realistic, etc., to show that they have something to follow. The most popular now is the realistic school, but I always feel that there is still some affectation. It is far inferior to the New Year couplet on the door of a thatched cottage at the foot of Dongshan Mountain in my hometown three years ago, which I passed on my way to worship at the ancestral graves: "Spring flowers, spring wine, spring wealth; Winter chicken, winter leg, winter sausage," which is more interesting for being realistic!

Love Notes

— Mu Zeqing

Love is like a non-term check; whether it can be cashed depends on the person's skill.

After the sweetness of being in love is produced, hesitation and terror come!

The first love of a smart person is secret; he is afraid that people will laugh at him for taking a blank check. The love of an ordinary person is public; he is deeply afraid that others will not know his luck.

The love of an old-fashioned woman is like a quiet lake, without tides. The love of a new-fashioned woman is like the price of bidding for gold, which often fluctuates.

In first love, one always wants to possess the other person. After possession, one wants to relax.

A family letter is worth ten thousand gold; a love letter is worth even more.

A woman does not like to love a writer; she is afraid of being used as material after a broken relationship.

When a woman and a man reach a passionate love, when they are close to the focus of love, she does not admit that she "loves" the man; she only admits that she is "fond" of him.

People in love have five illnesses: lovesickness, depression, neurosis, kidney disease, insomnia.

Marriage is love heading towards the grave; leaving is the same. Heaven brews the taste of sorrow into love, and starting again is a discount.

Between spiritual love and physical love, there is only a layer of mysterious thin paper; once broken, it is worthless.

Some people think that "love at first sight" is an emotional impulse, just a temporary game for both parties. However, the love that is completed by following the process of love, the foundation of which is also half built on sand.

For the sake of testing, a woman always looks for opportunities to torment a man. Sometimes the man feels more pain and more pleasure, and sometimes he feels unbearable. If a man can overcome or overcome the woman's temptations and torments, the woman can love him more wholeheartedly.

When a man and a woman cuddle, they only hate that time passes too quickly.

A lovesick person is praised by old-fashioned women, but new-fashioned women only find it pitiful and ridiculous.

A man with love experience is afraid of a woman with experience; both are veterans, and there is no true love and fun to be found. Women have the same mentality.

The "joy of love" at the first meeting has complicated thoughts; after the thoughts of respect and love, what remains is only "pity"!

The Four Northeast Company Commanders

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 25

Tearful Faces See Off People Returning Home to Distant Clans

Sandstorms All Night Outside the Border, Stationed in a Lonely City

Zi Qiang looked at his watch. Another ten minutes had passed. He said to Zhao Weng, "Do you have anything else to say?" Zhao Weng said, "I said everything I had to say yesterday. There's nothing more to say. Take care of yourself in everything." Jiang interjected from the side, "That's right, you must take care of yourself in everything." Zi Qiang didn't say anything. He took out his watch again to look at it. Zhao Weng said, "Have Xiao Lin come and carry your luggage with you. You go to the bus station first and wait. We'll all see you off to the station." Zi Qiang laughed, "How dare I accept that both of you old people see me off? It's fine if Gui Zhi sees me off." Zhao Weng was always considerate of his son. Since he said to let his beloved wife see him off alone, there might be another reason behind it. So he looked at Jiang and said, "It's okay if we don't see him off." Jiang never even said that she wanted to see him off. Zhao Weng said this, so naturally she accepted what she didn't agree to. Zi Qiang stood in the middle of the hall for a while, turned his head and looked into the courtyard twice, and still stopped. Gui Zhi saw that he wanted to leave but didn't want to, so she said, "It's still a few steps to the bus station, let's go first." So Zi Qiang called Zhao Weng "Dad" and Jiang "Old Lady," and then said "I'm leaving." He took off his hat, bowed deeply twice, put on his hat, suddenly stood at attention, turned around, and immediately took large steps, and walked out. As he walked, he didn't turn his head to look. He only heard the sound of leather shoes ringing, ringing all the way out the door. Xiao Lin carried the suitcase and bag, following behind. Gui Zhi quickly rushed forward, closely following behind him. Zi Qiang walked very quickly. When he reached the outside of the gate, his steps stopped. He said to Gui Zhi, "Did the two old people say anything?" Before Gui Zhi could answer him, someone called out from behind, "Zi Qiang, as soon as you get to the camp, write me a letter right away!" World Rare News

A Record of the Manila Carnival

— Yan Wenchou

For more than twenty years, the annual Carnival has seemed to bore the world. However, the Philippine government has repeatedly tried its best to promote it. One reason is that in this period of commercial decline, Manila, as the capital of the Philippines, can be embellished by this event. Visitors from all directions gather, and the market turns to be lively, just like taking a shot of stimulant, which can awaken the spirit. The other reason is that the citizens work hard all year round, suffer from the heat in the summer and the wetness in the rainy season, and this grand meeting in early spring serves as a spiritual adjustment, making women and children feel more energetic. And this year's Carnival has a more memorable value for our overseas Chinese.

The most attractive aspect of this grand event is the election of the Philippine Lady (i.e., the Flower Queen). For these twenty years, the old system of a few years ago has been restored. The right to the first election rests with the newspapers and magazines that have been registered, and the right to the second election rests with the shareholders. (Each share is ten yuan, and the association gives a beautiful badge, exempting the purchase of admission tickets, and has the right to enter the Grand Auditorium for five nights to watch various performances and dance.) More than ten years ago, the daughter of the Philippine Governor Harrison intended to be the successor to this imperial crown. As a result, there were many contestants, and the host compromised by dividing the crown into two queens, East and West, ruling in parallel. It can be seen that the glory of this sixteen-night throne is not easily obtained by ordinary young ladies. Unexpectedly, this year, a Chinese woman received the most votes for Philippine Lady. This is an unprecedented record for the Chinese Association, and a groundbreaking event in the overseas Chinese community. It is learned that the lady is the daughter of overseas Chinese merchant Chen Erheng, a student of the Music Department of the National University. Mr. Chen has many contacts in Philippine political circles, and his friends campaigned in many ways, which led to good results.

The entire meeting opened for sixteen nights, with four major parades. The first was a general parade, which could be joined by all agencies, societies, and shops, either in groups or with decorated floats. The Chinese Chamber of Commerce decorated a float depicting China thirty years ago and the two phenomena of China over the past thirty years. The judges announced that it won the first prize for its profound meaning. The second was an educational parade, and the scout troops from various overseas Chinese schools also participated. The float decorated by the China Zhizhi Education Association was at the end, and its intention was that the universal principles of the world are oppressed by airplanes and cannons, and the distance between the god of peace and the earth is still far away. The judges decided that it won the second prize for its gorgeous decoration. This can be said to be scratching where it doesn't itch.

Every night in the Grand Auditorium, the program is changed. On the afternoon of the 4th of this month at 4:00, it was Children's Day, and overseas Chinese schools from various countries were invited to join. The order of their performances was determined by lottery. First, there were more than two hundred female students from Japanese schools, wearing short clothes and blue skirts, standing in three concentric circles, performing the national flag dance, and their steps and music were very harmonious. The second was more than a hundred Filipino boys and girls, performing the pursuit of young men and women, performing various new-style dances. The third was Spanish boys and girls performing the ancient Three Princes fighting the bull, watching them after their victory, watching the men and women sing and dance happily. The fourth was our Qiao Girls' School performing Mulan joining the army. Due to time constraints (limited to twenty minutes), only Mulan General in ancient palace costume was performed, leading the soldiers in person to the front lines, with the shadows of swords and the light of knives, dancing gracefully. The fifth was American children playing villagers, surrounded by Red Indians, the whole family was wiped out, and the young girl was plundered by the Red Enemy, and the change of costumes did not indicate the ending. Overall, although the performances of various countries are rudimentary, each shows the national character. Japan has a military smell; Filipinos do not shed their pursuit of color; Spain still has a lot of religious color; and our country is antique. There were seven judges for the Miss Beauty election, four were female leaders, and three were the wives of the consuls of the West, China, and Japan. After the closing ceremony, it was announced that China won the first prize and Japan won the second prize. The judges' comments were that the costumes were elegant and symbolic, and promoted Eastern women's rights.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

The Two Major Crises Facing the National Goods Industry

— Xuan Wan

Everyone knows that our country is a country with backward production, so the ratio of production to consumption is only two to five. The phenomenon of "supply falling short of demand" has naturally created a trend of increasing reliance on foreign goods in recent years. We see that the countryside is bankrupt, and handicrafts are inevitably being eliminated by natural selection. Now, what we urgently need is to hope for the flourishing of domestic production enterprises, hoping to slightly make up for our own deficiencies and reverse the past decline. However, the painful reality shatters our ardent hopes. The so-called emerging industries are still fraught with difficulties. Looking around in the vast darkness, the future is full of thorns. The progress and stagnation of these industries can be imagined. Moreover, upon careful examination of their internal contradictions and conflicts, the various adverse phenomena are actually only going backward. To speak only of the current situation, there are two major crises facing the national goods industry. If these crises are not quickly avoided and continue, then they could prove fatal to national goods manufacturers.

(1) The Seriousness of Cutthroat Competition Among Companies in the Same Industry. People often call this a characteristic of Chinese people, but I say, let us rather call it the cause of a deadly ailment of Chinese people. Because of the manifestation of this inferior national character, I can categorically assert that it is the biggest obstacle to the progress of national goods. Often, a company's products and reputation are well-received and welcomed by society, but occasionally, because of the price reduction by one or two new factories, it is enough to ignite the fuse for the entire industry to trample on itself. All sorts of price wars, the manufacturing of inferior goods, and the clamor of "secondary brands" and "special prices" disturb the market. In severe cases, they violate the articles of association of trade associations, overturn previous resolutions, and commit outrageous actions, without end. And in the end, they inevitably resort to cutting corners and reducing materials due to cost concerns. As a result, society loses faith, gradually eliminates them, and they become beyond salvation.

(2) The Intensification of Foreign Goods Dumping. Imperialists, seeing the deepening of the world economic panic and the inability to overcome the crisis, with the market becoming increasingly narrow, overproduction, and rising unemployment, are trying as much as possible to shift the crisis losses to China within a possible range. Their dumping policies are becoming more and more severe, especially Japan, this ruthless demon. Recently, it has even combined government and business, using organized and planned strategies to carry out large-scale dumping. Not to mention other things, just the 2 million stones of Japanese rice transported to China, as reported the other day, is naturally enough to frighten us, who claim to "build the country on agriculture."

Exposing Mirror

— Tian Ran

Recently, the prices of headless light bulbs and wireless radios circulating on the market have been surprisingly low. In fact, most of them are Japanese goods. Sellers, with a conscience that has been obliterated, seek only profit. Purchasers, if they have any spirit, should be strictly cautious and must not, for the sake of the thought of "cheapness," harm the country and the people.

A customer who had business with customs officials came to say that customs officials recently discovered dozens of boxes of pencils unloaded at the Huishan Wharf, undoubtedly suspected of being Japanese goods. However, after opening them, they were found to be Dahua pencils. It was difficult to distinguish them from the original brand. The doubt in this case has not yet been clarified. He asked me to investigate it. Unfortunately, the Dahua factory is located in Hong Kong, and it is not known how it is. It can be seen how difficult it is to choose and purchase supplies.

A friend of mine purchased a Parker fountain pen at a certain place, but found it to be of poor quality after using it. He happened to meet a friend who said that it was a counterfeit pen made in Japan, with a price less than one-sixth of that of a Parker fountain pen, and the form and wording were difficult to distinguish. My friend rushed to consult An Nuo, the commercial counselor, who also strongly stated that it was a counterfeit. My friend was extremely indignant that he had obtained a counterfeit product at a high price and told the seller and the purchaser that they should pay close attention in the future. If discernment is unclear, it is still more reliable to trust domestic goods companies.

Amidst wind and rain, and with crises lurking everywhere, the future of our national goods is indeed not promising. At this critical moment, when disaster is imminent, how will those who advocate national goods deliberate on the situation, exhaust their wisdom, and strive to open up this serious situation and reverse the already collapsing tide?

The Patriotism of a Female Servant

— Zhao Xiaoyang

Zhang Ma labored diligently for a whole month and received four dollars in wages. She happily went to a certain road to buy some clothing material for the cold winter.

After buying it back, she proudly showed it to her mistress!

"Madam, I got a bargain! This clothing material only costs six cents a foot, and the pattern is not bad!"

It happened that Qian Jie saw it! She immediately discovered the traces on the clothing material!

"Zhang Ma! You bought foreign goods! That's why the price is so cheap. Look! Isn't there a very clear (Made in Japan) label stuck on the edge of this clothing material?"

Qian Jie's eyesight is indeed much better! "What? I clearly bought it in the XX store!" Zhang Ma was somewhat suspicious. She carefully looked at the clothing material and felt that the weaving was very simple.

"That's right, you've been tricked! Let me tell you! These kinds of shops specialize in this kind of speculative business. On the surface, they loudly promote national goods, but in reality, they are constantly importing enemy goods! It's really heartbreaking to talk about!"

Qian Jie explained to her in a torrent of words.

"Ah! Miss, I don't want to make this clothing material! But it's a bit wasteful to throw it away, so I'll just use it as a diaper for Xiao Bao! Alas! These unscrupulous merchants who disregard shame will eventually fail one day!"

Zhang Ma's full of patriotism aroused Fu Jie's infinite gratitude. Then, Qian Jie accompanied her to a nearby national goods store to buy some domestically produced Free Ni clothing material. Although the price was relatively more expensive, the quality was extremely strong!

I think, a female servant who is illiterate actually has such a sincere patriotism, which makes me feel extremely admired and respectful. I wonder what several modern ladies would think when they heard this!
