The Shenbao Local Supplement

Idle Talk

On the Issue of Divorce

— Nai Shuo

| I Support Divorce, But Do Not Advocate for It |

The general public, upon hearing the word "divorce," immediately deems it "heretical and rebellious," which is, in fact, a misconception. Indeed, divorce has often carried a tragic connotation in Chinese history. However, we must understand that this is not inherent to divorce itself, but rather a product of the social system of the past and its trappings. Conversely, divorce is the very means to resolve tragedies between men and women; it is the gospel for modern relationships. This may sound surprising to some.

Originally, according to the doctrines of those conservative Confucian scholars, divorce was indeed "heretical and rebellious" because their societal mindset was deeply rooted in ritual and ethics. The creed for women was to remain faithful to one husband until death, and the dogma of marriage was that divorce should not occur unless there were offenses such as violating chastity or disrespecting elders. Naturally, in such a time, if you wanted a divorce, your wife must have committed one of the seven great sins of women, and society would exert its power of sanction, subjecting the woman to all sorts of abuse. Moreover, such women lacked skills to independently earn a living, and their families, apart from a meager dowry, could not offer any economic support. The outcome of divorce was indeed somewhat tragic. We do acknowledge that there is some validity in the sentiments of those conservative Confucian scholars.

However, this remains fragmented. If we contemplate with a calm mind, we will still discover the foolishness and pitiableness of those conservative Confucian scholars. When observing or thinking about anything, one should always stand before it, gaze at it, and allow its true and concrete shadow to be etched in our hearts, leaving a profound impression. Then, let us carefully ponder. Only in this way can we delve into the core of the matter and fully understand its true nature.

Thus, we turn back to examine the current issue of divorce. In the union of men and women, why does the phenomenon of divorce occur? To think this way is to confront the real aspect of the problem. Further expanding, consider the fall of celestial bodies, the detachment of ripe fruit from branches, the division of political factions, and the battles between allied nations. Continuing to examine their causes, we can certainly understand that their separation is due to intense conflicts arising during their respective developmental processes. When these conflicts reach a point where there is no possibility of resolution, they cannot but separate. Following the same pattern, we can find the contradictions in the union of men and women. We know that during the stage of courtship, emotions often easily mask individuality. When we observe our beloved, we always strive to uncover her (or his) virtues and pay no attention to her flaws. Later, because everyone feels that the other person is full of virtues and everyone feels satisfied, they unite. In married life, whether man or woman, they no longer cautiously suppress their own individuality or inherent quirks as they did during courtship. This is where the issues of compatibility and incompatibility of personalities, and the ability or inability to sustain virtues arise. For example, if you are a sensitive person with a literary hobby, but your husband is a science student whose mind only thinks in terms of "W + Y = X," you will naturally become estranged due to the difference in hobbies. It's as if when your husband comes home, you hope he will embrace you for a while; before going to sleep, you want him to tell you romantic words, but your husband considers it the most boring and dull thing. It's as if in your conversation with your husband, you talk about how profound a certain poem or novel is, but your husband only talks about things in the dissection room. It's also as if you are neat and sociable, while your husband is slovenly and reclusive. These are naturally the places where your personalities do not match. At this time, if you live together longer, the development of your personalities will only further distance you. Thus, a couple who were originally the closest and most intimate people now become the most distant and unfamiliar union. In such alienated and indifferent lives, deeper pain will naturally arise. No matter which standpoint you take, no one would hope for a painful life to remain with them forever. On the contrary, they are most willing to fight for happiness. If we are in such a painful life of a male-female union, then what other option do we have besides divorce? Therefore, when I talk about the issue of divorce, I have considerable support for it. My support is because in nature, forced unions and separations are impossible, and in the human world, forced unions and separations are also impossible. If a union is impossible, separation is inevitable. If one does not follow the dictates of this natural law, there will only be endless suffering. As for divorce being disadvantageous to women, the facts are not entirely true. The so-called disadvantages generally include the difficulty of remarriage and the burden of children. Regarding the difficulty of remarriage, people generally believe that the value of a virgin is higher than that of a non-virgin; a remarried woman is always considered flawed jade. This, of course, is not worth a scoff from those with knowledge; it is the most vulgar thing. The central point of their theory is nothing more than that virgins are most likely to possess a firm sense of chastity, while remarried women seem to have lost the guarantee of their chastity. Is the concept of chastity directly tied to the hymen? Are women without a hymen necessarily more promiscuous and unfaithful in love than virgins? This is a pathetic joke. I feel that besides considering such opinions vulgar and unbearable, there is nothing else to say. As for the burden of children, I feel that this is a non-issue. Because in the tenets of divorce, the party who initiates the divorce is bound to bear the living expenses of the children. This burden of living expenses is certainly not a form of social punishment, but a personal obligation that should be fulfilled. For the sake of liberating oneself from the pain of life and breaking free from mental shackles, it is certainly an obligation that should be fulfilled.

Conclusion: I support divorce, but I do not advocate for it.

In the Dormitory

— Mei Jun

The autumn breeze is so clear and refreshing. In this near-rural area, it is especially filled with a serene and secluded atmosphere, but it inevitably seems somewhat desolate and bleak. The waves of my heart, as still as dead water, often surge with inexplicable tides, faintly seeming to sob. Is it depression?

In middle school, I eagerly longed for the so-called sacred halls of the university. I used all my efforts to fulfill my wish, and actually stepped into the gate of the university, listening to lectures with excitement, curiosity, and fear. However, the beginning was particularly uncomfortable. The gazes of the male students were even more terrifying than those of the hooligans on the street. Whether it was sharp, or silent, or even seemingly gentle, they were all particularly piercing. Loud or low voices only made me feel that their every move contained a kind of distasteful and terrifying flavor that was unapproachable. A new life full of enthusiasm and hope had become faintly dull after just over a month. I can't say what the reason is!

I have no close friends to confide in and vent my endless complaints. I can only occasionally meet with my diary to vent my frustrations and slightly soothe my mind.

I am trying hard to be calm and clear, but the surrounding atmosphere is suffocating, and some phenomena are truly strange.

During the day, I already feel bored. I thought the night would be more comfortable, but the university dormitory, meant for studying, is as noisy as a teahouse or theater in Shanghai, making people weary. Unfortunately, our female dormitory is adjacent to the male dormitory. At night, noisy sounds often come from the male dormitory: not clear and melodious singing, but rather out-of-tune shouting, and every sound seems to have some deep meaning, a deep meaning that makes one vaguely aware of something terrifying. Mixed with playful and sharp laughter and shouts, the phonograph is also turned on. Sometimes Cantonese and Beijing opera tunes are mixed together in a discordant way, and one can't make out anything, just a bunch of unpleasant noises. The sound of mahjong tiles can almost be heard, but not very clearly. It has become customary to have this show every night. I wonder how they read their books, and what the school authorities are doing. With such a school spirit, one can't help but think that the sanctity of education has gone bankrupt.

Tonight, I heard their vulgar song: "...As long as your heart..."

It really makes me feel embarrassed for them. The more cultured one in the union can play the piano, but it always feels out of tune, even though I don't understand the piano. Those sounds of theirs are, of course, annoying, but they also seem to have some kind of power, making one feel particularly depressed. Many female students are so disturbed that they have no heart to study and can only sing softly. Sometimes I am really too bored and will unconsciously join them for a few sounds, but it is always tasteless. Where is my soul going?

Last night's strange phenomenon really disgusted me: two classmates in the same room seemed to be laughing and joking freely, as if something had provoked them. It was after dusk, around 9 pm, in the cool and pleasant night air, I was quietly reviewing my homework when the giggling and surprised movements of the two female classmates on the window-side bed suddenly disturbed me. I looked up and saw a beam of white light from a flashlight shining into the room from the dark outside the window, directly onto the table near the window. I was very surprised at first, but in an instant, I understood that this light was coming from the male dormitory across the way. I turned and was suddenly stunned. Looking at the window, I could vaguely see a few shadowy figures moving and wriggling in the windows of the male dormitory across the way, as if they were doing something. I was really angry and burst out cursing at these so-called high-class hooligans of the university. They were also laughing and gesturing as they criticized. Without waiting for their opinions, I reached out and closed the window, but before it was fully closed, the male students across the way let out a particularly loud and victorious laugh. This burst of laughter pierced my heart, and I felt suddenly that my cheeks were burning, and my body was rushing faster, unable to sit still, feeling ashamed, embarrassed, and terrible. Lying down, I just tossed and turned, unable to fall asleep, the gentle quilt and comfortable smell all disappeared. Thinking about it carefully, I felt more distressed and disappointed, making me unable to doubt this kind of life.

After the lights were turned off, I was still vaguely tossing and turning, unable to sleep, and gradually it seemed much quieter.

When I woke up, I don't know why my mood was even more chaotic. Holding my head, I felt oppressed and empty. The night bell rang, cutting off my heartstrings...one o'clock...three o'clock...

When I got up in the morning, the female classmate who slept by the window also told me that after the window was closed, she saw the light from the flashlight hovering on the glass of the window several times again. If it wasn't flashing, one might have suspected it was moonlight. Perhaps the female classmate was also disturbed a little in the night, so she also put on a serious face and scolded those boring college students. How barbaric and terrifying is this behavior! I added another layer of feeling insulted in my heart.

Movie Stars and Dancers

— Jun

Previously, we always felt there was a distinction between movie stars and dancers. Their social status and value were incomparable. At least, movie stars were slightly better than dancers, and they left a more fulfilling impression in the minds of the general public. But now, the reality is far from that. Film merchants purely adhere to a profit-driven ideology, making use of movie stars' thighs and breasts as advertising gimmicks to attract business. A quick glance at the daily newspapers reveals large, sensational advertisements that are everywhere. This kind of sexual fetishism is not unique to China. The film industry in Europe and America has even gone further. In this capitalist society, any profession is inevitably commodified. Film merchants, in order to increase their business profits, compete to imitate each other, creating novelties and eccentricities. The more vulgar, the better, to cater to the low-level tastes of the petty bourgeoisie. As a result, sensational productions are produced in large quantities, and the film industry's atmosphere becomes naturally foul-smelling.

And it is undeniable that female stars are happy to sacrifice their beauty. It is precisely because female stars can sacrifice their beauty that wealthy bosses do not worry about being unable to make money. Female stars have fallen to this level, only fifty steps away from dancers who embrace for a dollar. We can cite one or two things to illustrate. Earlier, there was the case of Li Li, a dancer from Da Hua Dance Hall, who went on to the silver screen, but ended up returning to the jazz music scene to live her original life. Recently, there was the case of Liang Saizhen, who once surprised people by switching from a career on the silver screen to becoming a dancer. They all say that it is because the income of a star is far less than that of a dancer, and to satisfy their needs, they only have this one path. These are all words of sorrow, frank words. In fact, whether it is from star to dancer, or from dancer to star, it is nothing more than a change in an individual's living environment. There is nothing to be surprised about. Moreover, everyone's thoughts and actions cannot fundamentally escape the control of economic power. In order to seek a more comfortable life and change their lifestyle, regardless of how the new lifestyle is changed, we cannot superficially decide that their behavior is wrong or degenerate, but should criticize it based on objective conditions. How can we simply criticize the many women who run to the streets at night to sell their bodies and smiles as willingly degrading themselves? Those who fall are not willingly degraded. But objective facts make it so.

Honestly, movie stars and dancers are one and two, and two and one. The wave of the world economic panic has swept the globe, and the decline of the film industry is getting worse every day. The stars engaged in film are deeply aware of the shaking of their status and the misfortune of the future. Even the general stars of Hollywood, who have the highest salaries in the world, are experiencing life's panic, let alone others. As a maze for the leisure class, as long as the gentleman class and bourgeoisie do not collapse, the dance hall will not be eliminated for a day. In the long run, the general stars who have no way out may all flock to the path of becoming a dancer, who knows.

The Threshold of Fighting

— Tao Dan

"Fighting" seems barbaric, but in this modern world where only power exists and there is no justice, it is better to use force to gain some advantage. At the same time, "fighting" is also necessary. When resentful, wanting someone to be patient is likely to cause health problems. So, in the past, a group of rich masters and ladies - and there are still some now - bought many slaves in advance, ready to use them as a frame to vent their anger when they were unhappy. So, I say: When you can hit someone, why not hit them? However, there is a threshold for hitting, and those who are not proficient in the threshold will not only fail to hit anyone, but may also be beaten instead. Those who hit people, can't you be careful?

Fighting has its own goal. Those who hit people must not overestimate their abilities and act rashly. You must understand the principle of "know yourself and know your enemy, and you will never be defeated." You must have the confidence, and you should first consider whether you can withstand his counterattack. So, for those who are taller and bigger, it is better to adopt a "long-term resistance" method, taking a step back as a good strategy. So-called calm attitude, calm response, avoid eating immediate losses. Conversely, when your fists are itchy, seeing consumptives, opium addicts, etc., or even women and children, those small and weak nationalities, you may as well roll up your sleeves, pull out your fists, and show off your skills, and I guarantee that you will not suffer losses.

Speaking of fighting, you can't help but think of cursing. To hit someone, you must first curse, and this is also reasonable. Like when two sides go to war, before mobilizing troops, there must first be a telegram declaration, listing the other side's crimes, so that others will believe that we are sacrificing for justice. Cursing before fighting is the same principle. Then, the spectators can all criticize the other party's shortcomings, saying that you are reasonable. Even if he really doesn't have much wrong, you may as well catch him on a small matter - it doesn't matter if it doesn't concern you, just make a big fuss over a small issue, and speak nonsense as you please, as long as you curse loudly enough.

Maybe you are afraid before you start, which is simply the behavior of a coward. In fact, there is no need to worry. Anyway, if you lose, just put on a straight face, shake hands with the other party, and congratulate him on his success. To the audience? You may as well say: "Victory or defeat is commonplace in war, why bother mentioning it? Moreover, failure is the mother of success, look at this day next year." Of course, it is still best not to come on this day next year. A great man has ambitions in all directions, and why can't he avoid it from afar. Further, if you really sacrifice your life for hitting someone, there is no reason for that. Sixteen years later, you will still be a good man?

Finally: I declare first! Although I have no experience in fighting, I dare say that this whole threshold is theoretically established; if you don't believe it, you may as well try it. As for fighting and causing a lawsuit involving human life, that is because your fist is too effective, and I cannot be responsible.

Amateur Mailbox

Does This Also Warrant Suicide!

Editor:

I am from Beijing, and I have a difficult problem that requires guidance. Please answer it in the Amateur Mailbox column.

A weak girl, Jia, is nineteen years old this year. When she was very, very young, her parents betrothed her to a relative, Yi, as his wife. Later, they often met and found that the fiancé was very rude, especially his stubborn temperament. Therefore, since the engagement, she has never had her fiancé in her mind. She is extremely sad and has always had thoughts of death. She insists that no matter what, she cannot marry him. Yi is my closest friend, and I have considerable feelings for him. So, I previously advised Jia not to resort to extremes, but to no effect. However, Jia is very fond of me, often expressing her willingness to cancel the engagement with Yi and marry me. Because I am fond of her, and after careful observation in all aspects, I feel that she has a good conscience. Coupled with the fact that we are getting closer day by day, we have recently reached the peak of love. Her parents also agree with me, and we two have verbally engaged. Her parents also agree. If I didn't know Yi, there would certainly be no problem. However, if I don't marry Jia, Jia will in fact have to find another partner, that is, force a marriage and divorce in the end: because Jia was looking for a partner before she loved me, and she had already decided that she would rather die than marry, in order to clarify her name and plan another. So, I feel that in fact I have not wronged Yi. However, if I tell Yi, I am not a friend. But if I leave Jia because of this, then I still wronged Jia. I am now in a very difficult situation, loving Jia but afraid of wronging Yi, so I have the idea of ​​loathing the world. I opened a room at the China Grand Hotel in the capital, ready to die to thank Jia and Yi. However, I am a weak person. After two days here, I am still hesitant. Seeing your newspaper's Amateur Mailbox, I have the idea of ​​stealing my life. If you can give me a good idea, there may still be hope for survival. I hope you will reply soon, reply in the newspaper, my surname is Cheng, I will not announce my name, then I will be grateful, and the kindness will be the same as rebuilding. There are also three small questions, please answer them together.

(1) Should I put love for Jia above the sacredness of love? Or friendship for Yi?

(2) If love should be prioritized, of course this friend must be sacrificed, and there should be no contact with him. But I still want to contact him. Is there a good way?

(3) Jia and Yi are both my friends. If this difficult problem was asked by Jia, then how should Jia treat Yi and me? Please put yourself in Jia's shoes and guide her.

Cheng Qi, February 20th, at the Capital China Grand Hotel

Answer: Mr. Cheng, don't commit suicide. There is no need to commit suicide. Moreover, people don't need to commit suicide at all. Although the method offered to you by the editor may not be the best method, as long as you try your best to find it, there is always a method. Why do you have to think about suicide?

Marriage should always be based on love, which is a fact, not an ideal. The "girl" you requested, she doesn't love "Yi" at all, so if she marries "Yi", she will certainly be ruining herself, not to mention that...

Brother Mao and Sister Bao Travel the World

— Meng

Tricked into the slave traders' village. A granny opens the door: the granny has a red nose, and is very happy to see them.

The slave traders are going to kidnap and buy people, but instead lock them two in the wall: Brother Mao feels strange; Sister Bao is scared and curses.

The slave traders open the box, and the granny looks at the goods: everyone says that this kind of goods is very good: everyone can surely get a few!

Brother Mao and Sister Bao are locked in a dark room together: they are hungry and anxious.
